21-23 Point Modern Decklists
============================



 Posted in **Event Coverage**
 on February 7, 2016 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/authorpic_EventCoverageStaff.jpg)
By Event Coverage Staff











A total of 40 players earned 21 or 22 points in the Modern rounds of Pro Tour *Oath of the Gatewatch*. There were 38 players who earned 21 points (7-3) from Modern and two who earned 22 points (7-2-1). No one earned 23 points.




---

#### The following players finished with 22 points (7-2-1) in Modern:







#### Shuhei Nakamura: Colorless Eldrazi


##### 




![](https://web.archive.org/web/20160726232508im_/http://magic.wizards.com/sites/all/modules/features/wiz_bean_content_deck_list/icons/decklist_download.png)
